By our very nature we were subject to Godâ€™s anger, just like everyone else.  But God is so rich in mercy, and he loved us so much, that even though we were dead because of our sins, he gave us life when he raised Christ from the dead. (It is only by Godâ€™s grace that you have been saved!) For he raised us from the dead along with Christ and seated us with him in the heavenly realms because we are united with Christ Jesus. So God can point to us in all future ages as examples of the incredible wealth of his grace and kindness toward us, as shown in all he has done for us who are united with Christ Jesus.

I just noticed something. This track is right before "Won't Cry." In this song Jay is taking the perspective of the person moving on from the relationship with some regret and hoping the best for the one left behind. In "Won't Cry" Jay takes the perspective of the person who has been left behind but then realizes that the party moving on did it for their benefit. I wonder if these two songs are intended to be a pair.
